 6 lakhs increased from Rs 4
 5 lakh rupee kar di gai he

 The Reserve Bank of India (RBI) on Tuesday announced the elimination of fees levied on payments before the maturity of a floating interest rate home loan
 rigerv bank ne is sambandh main ek adhisuchana jari kii
 The bank statement said that due to this fee, loan holders cannot use cheap resources
 tippaniyan According to the statement, the Reserve Bank of India had recently voluntarily removed the fee on premature repayment of temporary interest rate home loan, after which there was a need to establish parity for all banks
 bayaan main kaha gaya, "isliye yah tay kiya gaya he ki tatkaal prabhaav se bainkon ko asthai byaaj vaale rin ke punarbhugtan par shulk lagane kii anumati nahin di jaaegi
 " rigerv bank ne is sambandh main ek adhisuchana jari kii
 The bank statement said that due to this fee, loan holders cannot use cheap resources
 tippaniyan According to the statement, the Reserve Bank of India had recently voluntarily removed the fee on premature repayment of temporary interest rate home loan, after which there was a need to establish parity for all banks
 bayaan main kaha gaya, "isliye yah tay kiya gaya he ki tatkaal prabhaav se bainkon ko asthai byaaj vaale rin ke punarbhugtan par shulk lagane kii anumati nahin di jaaegi
 " bayaan ke mutabik rigerv bank ne kai bainkon ne haal main swechha se asthai byaaj dar vaale awaas rin kii samay purv adaayagi par shulk hataa diya tha, jiske baad sabhi bainkon ke liye samanta sthapit karne kii jarurat thi
 The statement said, "it has therefore been decided that banks will not be allowed to levy fees on the repayment of temporary interest loans with immediate effect
